Management believes this non-GAAP information is useful for investors, when considered in conjunction with Gilead&#8217;s GAAP financial statements, because management uses such information internally for its operating, budgeting and financial planning purposes. Non-GAAP information is not prepared under a comprehensive set of accounting rules and should only be used to supplement an understanding of Gilead&#8217;s operating results as reported under GAAP. Non-GAAP measures may be defined and calculated differently by other companies in the same industry. style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Foster City, CA, February&#160;11, 2025</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> - Gilead Sciences, Inc. (Nasdaq&#58; GILD) announced today its results of operations for the fourth quarter and full year</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">2024. </font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;Gilead delivered another exceptionally strong full year and fourth quarter, with growth in our base business product sales of 8% for 2024 and 13% year-over-year for the fourth quarter,&#8221; said Daniel O&#8217;Day, Gilead&#8217;s Chairman and Chief Executive Officer. &#8220;From this foundation of commercial strength, we are planning for the potential launch of lenacapavir for HIV PrEP in Summer 2025, with its unique opportunity to extend the reach of HIV prevention. This potential in HIV, along with our strong and diverse portfolio, and improved operational efficiencies, positions Gilead to deliver increasing patient impact and compelling shareholder returns in the years ahead.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Fourth Quarter 2024 Financial Results</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Total fourth quarter 2024 revenue increased 6% to $7.6 billion compared to the same period in 2023, primarily due to higher sales in HIV, as well as in Oncology and Liver Disease, partially offset by lower sales of Veklury&#174; (remdesivir). </font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Diluted Earnings Per Share (&#8220;EPS&#8221;) increased to $1.42 in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to $1.14 in the same period in 2023, primarily driven by lower costs of goods sold, higher product sales and lower acquired in-process research and development (&#34;IPR&#38;D&#34;) expenses, partially offset by higher operating expenses as well as unrealized losses on equity investments in 2024 compared to gains in 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Non-GAAP diluted EPS increased to $1.90 in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to $1.72 in the same period in 2023. The increase was primarily driven by higher product sales and lower acquired IPR&#38;D expenses, partially offset by higher operating expenses.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">As of December 31, 2024, Gilead had $10.0 billion of cash, cash equivalents and marketable debt securities compared to $8.4 billion as of December&#160;31, 2023. </font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font cash flow. </font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font aggregate principal amount of $3.5 billion, paid cash dividends of $973 million and utilized $350 million to repurchase common stock.</font></div><div id="i97c587a4bc2a4c4fbcb2c4efc411a9a3_4"></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Fourth Quarter Disease.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">HIV</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> (FTC 200mg&#47;TAF 25mg) sales increased 21% to $616 million in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to the same period in 2023, primarily driven by higher demand, higher average realized price and favorable inventory dynamics. </font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> portfolio sales increased 4% to $719 million in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to the same period in 2023. This was primarily driven by the launch of Livdelzi&#174; (seladelpar) in primary biliary cholangitis (&#8220;PBC&#8221;), and increased demand in products for chronic hepatitis B virus (&#8220;HBV&#8221;) and chronic hepatitis delta virus (&#8220;HDV&#8221;), partially offset by lower demand and average realized price in products for chronic hepatitis C virus (&#8220;HCV&#8221;).</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Veklury </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to the same period in 2023, primarily driven by lower rates of COVID-19 related hospitalizations, particularly in the United States.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font period in 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font to the same period in 2023, primarily driven by higher average realized price and increased demand outside of the United States, partially offset by lower demand in the United States.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font to the same period in 2023, reflecting increased demand outside of the United States, offset by lower demand in the United States.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font 2024 compared to the same period in 2023, primarily driven by increased demand in all regions, as well as higher average realized price.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font in the same period in 2023, primarily driven by prior year restructuring expenses related to changes in our manufacturing strategy. Non-GAAP product gross margin was 86.7% in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to 86.1% in the same period in 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Research and development (&#8220;R&#38;D&#8221;) expenses were $1.6 billion in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to $1.4 billion in the same period in 2023, primarily due to incremental investments and clinical activities across our portfolio and the impact of a prior year valuation adjustment to the MYR-related contingent consideration that did not repeat. Non-GAAP R&#38;D expenses were $1.6 billion in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to $1.5 billion</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">in the same period in 2023, primarily due to incremental investments and clinical activities across our portfolio.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Acquired IPR&#38;D expenses were $(11) million in the fourth quarter 2024, reflecting expenses related to the Terray Therapeutics, Inc. (&#8220;Terray&#8221;) and Tubulis GmbH (&#8220;Tubulis&#8221;) collaborations, offset by a favorable adjustment related to the CymaBay Therapeutics, Inc. (&#8220;CymaBay&#8221;) acquisition.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Selling, general and administrative (&#8220;SG&#38;A&#8221;) and non-GAAP SG&#38;A expenses were $1.9 billion in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to $1.6 billion in the same period in 2023, primarily driven by a litigation accrual and higher sales and marketing spending, including launch preparation activities for lenacapavir for the investigational use of HIV pre-exposure prophylaxis (&#8220;PrEP&#8221;) as well as for Livdelzi.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">The effective tax rate (&#8220;ETR&#8221;) was 17.8% in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to 14.3% in the same period in 2023, primarily due to prior year settlements with tax authorities and non-taxable unrealized gains and losses on equity investments. Non-GAAP ETR was 19.2% in the fourth quarter 2024 compared to 17.1% in the same period in 2023, primarily due to prior year settlements with tax authorities.</font></div><div Infection (&#8220;HIV Glasgow 2024&#8221;). This included full results from the Phase 3 PURPOSE 2 trial evaluating investigational twice-yearly lenacapavir for HIV prevention among cisgender men and gender-diverse people, with data published in the </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">New England Journal of Medicine</font><font style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font Administration (&#8220;FDA&#8221;), as well as a marketing authorization application and an EU-Medicines for All application to the European Medicines Agency (&#8220;EMA&#8221;), for twice-yearly lenacapavir for HIV prevention. </font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font Year,&#8221; based in part on the PURPOSE 1 and PURPOSE 2 trial results.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font The use of Trodelvy in ES-SCLC is investigational. </font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Entered into a single-asset focused collaboration, license, and option agreement with Tubulis to develop an antibody-drug conjugate candidate for a solid tumor target using Tubulis&#8217; Tubutecan and Alco5 platforms.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Inflammation</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Received a positive opinion from the EMA&#8217;s Committee for Medicinal Products for Human Use recommending seladelpar for the treatment of PBC in combination with ursodeoxycholic acid (&#8220;UDCA&#8221;) in adults who have an inadequate response to UDCA alone, or as monotherapy in those unable to tolerate UDCA.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Received marketing authorization from the Medicines and Healthcare products Regulatory Agency in the UK for seladelpar for treatment of PBC, including pruritus, in adults in combination with UDCA who have an inadequate response to UDCA alone, or as monotherapy in those unable to tolerate UDCA.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.53pt">Presented new data evaluating seladelpar in PBC at the American Association for the Study of Liver Diseases&#8217; The Liver Meeting. This included longer-term follow-up data from the ASSURE trial, as well as additional analyses from the RESPONSE trial. </font></div><div Management believes non-GAAP information is useful for investors, when considered in conjunction with Gilead&#8217;s GAAP financial information, because management uses such information internally for its operating, budgeting and financial planning purposes. Non-GAAP information is not prepared under a comprehensive set of accounting rules and should only be used to supplement an understanding of Gilead&#8217;s operating results as reported under GAAP. Non-GAAP financial information generally excludes acquisition-related expenses including amortization of acquired intangible assets and other items that are considered unusual or not representative of underlying trends of Gilead&#8217;s business, fair value adjustments of equity securities and discrete and related tax charges or benefits associated with such exclusions as well as changes in tax-related laws and guidelines, transfers of intangible assets between certain legal entities, and legal entity restructurings. The company is committed to advancing innovative medicines to prevent and treat life-threatening diseases, including HIV, viral hepatitis, COVID-19, cancer and inflammation. Gilead operates in more than 35 countries worldwide, with headquarters in Foster City, California.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Statements included in this press release that are not historical in nature are forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995.
